Very cool spot, great one of a kind business. Plenty hair products for curly hair, there even is a hair salon inside. Also a lot of great skin care products, from jojoba oil, coconut oil, almond oil, apple cider vinegar, books on black history and culture, spiritual merchandise, like incense and sage and books, music. The people are very cool every time. Very one-love one-world people, has a very spiritual culturally proud and forward thinking vibe, I love it. Smells so nice too, when you just drop by.
I always load up on skin care oils in here, and have always splurged on various small souvenirs also, they have jewelry and small purses, accessories like that. Love the shae butter balls, they are about a fist sized!<//Review>

This place was open for in dining, but still had covid restrictions for seating. Still there were alot of people in there to enjoy. Sushi bar is still not opened. The food was good, service was good, but could of been better. It took them awhile to take our initial order. We had the all you can eat dinner version ($28.00), I got the lobster popcorn, and from the picture, I didnt notice that it was on a roll, so aside from our sushi order, that order came with cut rolls of rice and it was to much. All the sushi was delicious, I also ordered a rainbow roll, shrimp crunch with eel, and spicy tuna crunch rolls.< /text>
